WHAT WAS THE PRIMARY DIAGNOSIS OF THE FIRST AGENT CONSULTED ABOUT CHILD'S
HEALTH?

SURVEY:  LONGITUDINAL 5      SUBJECT:     CHILD HEALTH CARE
SAMPLE:  2695                FILE LEVEL:  HOUSEHOLD / SAMPLE WOMAN

 1 - Person consulted prescribed 'western' medicine because child is sick
     (fever, cough, colds, diarrhea, allergy, measles, etc.)
 2 - Child has sprain and was massaged (Napiang or nalisa ug gihilot ang bata)
 3 - Treated or prescribed treatment for infected umbilical cord
 4 - Child is healthy/all right
 5 - Child is fit for immunization (i.e. DPT, Polio, etc.)
 6 - Recommended oral rehydration (i.e. Oresol, Pedialyte, etc.)
 7 - Prescribed/Applied inhaled steam, Eucalyptus oil/Enema/Hot/Cold compress
 8 - Prescribed exposure to sea breeze/sunlight
 9 - Recommended fruit juices i.e. lemonsito juice or oral fluids or water
10 - Recommended vaporub (Vicks, etc.) or ointment (Aziete de Manzanilla, etc.)
     for child's chest, throat, back or stomach
11 - Recommended that atis, asiotes or other medicinal leaves (smoked, pounded,
     etc.) be applied to affected area with or without kerosene or coconut oil
12 - Prescribed/Gave 'special local concoction' to child for drinking
     (i.e. young atis leaves, gabon, white orchid flowers, bagayana,
     suwa sa cogon, granada roots soaked in water over a period of time)
13 - Recommended/Applied kerosene, vinegar or coconut oil on affected area
14 - Recommended hospitalization
15 - Diagnosis only, no recommendation
16 - Gi-oracionan, includes "tot-ho"
17 - Recommended vitamins since child is vitamin deficient
18 - Others (SPECIFY)
19 - Recommended change in infant formula/diet because child is allergic
-8 - NR/DK
-9 - NA
